PURPLE PROTOCOL - ENHANCED NODE DYNAMICS:
───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
1. Nodes spawn in dynamic clusters every 1.5 seconds
2. Nodes exhibit constant movement with speed between 2-6
3. Collision triggers cryptographic signature synthesis (10-bit)
4. CATALYST NODES: Spawn with 25% chance every 15 normal nodes
5. Catalyst nodes flicker between multiple colors
6. When two catalyst nodes collide, they attempt 20 guesses at once
7. Normal nodes that interact with catalysts get double guesses next time
8. Green nodes (verified) don't interact with catalysts
9. Verified pairs auto-purge after 4 seconds to prevent system overload
10. System terminates upon signature match
